Boyaa Privacy Policy
This Privacy Policy will be effective from May 25, 2009.
Please read Boyaa's Privacy Policy before using Boyaa's services because it will tell you how we collect, store, use and disclose your personal information when providing these services to you.
If you have questions or complaints regarding our Privacy Policy or practices, please see Contact Us: cs@boyaa.com
Table of Contents
â€¢	1.Introduction
â€¢	2.European GDPR update
â€¢	3.Information we collect and how we collect it
â€¢	4.How we use the information we collect
â€¢	5.How we share your information
â€¢	6.How to access, update and manage your information
â€¢	7.Privacy policies of linked third-party services and advertisers
â€¢	8.Our policies concerning children
â€¢	9.How long we keep your information
â€¢	10.Security of your information
â€¢	11.Changes to our Privacy Policy
â€¢	12.Contact Us
1.Introduction
Boyaa develops and publishes social games for the web and mobile devices. "Boyaa," or "we" or "us" refers to Boyaa Online Game Development (Shenzhen) Co., Ltd. and Shenzhen Dong Fang BoYa Technology Co., Ltd. in this Privacy Policy. The Boyaa Corporate Family means Boyaa's subsidiaries, parent companies, joint ventures and other corporate entities under common ownership and/or any of their agents, consultants, employees, officers and directors.
This Privacy Policy applies whenever you play our games or otherwise access any of our other products, services, content, Boyaa.com and/or the other domains provided by Boyaa, together referred to as "Services." This Privacy Policy describes:
â€¢	what information we collect, how we collect it, and why
â€¢	how we use that information and with whom we share it
â€¢	how you can access and update that information
â€¢	the choices you can make about how we collect, use, and share your information
â€¢	how we protect the information we store about you
If you do not want Boyaa to collect, store, use or share your information in the ways described in this Privacy Policy, you may not play Boyaa's games or use Boyaa's Services.
2.European GDPR update:
2.1 What are Boyaa's duties under the GDPR?
Protect personal data using appropriate security.
Notify authorities of personal data breaches.
Obtain appropriate consents for processing data.
Keep records detailing data processing.
Train privacy personnel and employees.
Audit and update data policies.
Employ a Data Protection Officer.
2.2 What can players do if they are located in the EU:
Players can access or request deletion of their personal information by submitting a request through our customer service channel.
Please be advised that by deleting your personal data, all game progress, and virtual goods or currency paid for and/or earned across ALL Boyaa games will be terminated
Players can correct or update their personal information
Players can request Boyaa to restrict the processing of their personal information
Players can demand portability of their personal information
Players can opt-out of marketing communications
Players can withdraw their prior consent at any time.
Players have the right to complain to a data protection authority.
2.3 Boyaa as a data controller
When Boyaa collects personal data and determines the purposes and means of processing that personal data, it acts as a data controller. To manage the information Boyaa receives about players from a third-party application or platform, like Facebook, Apple or Google, players will need to follow the third-party instructions for updating your information and changing your privacy settings.
2.4 Processing according to users consent
Any data that a user put into our systems will only be processed following playersâ€™ permission, as described in this Privacy policy.
2.5 Future improvements and commitments
We have already implemented most of the GDPR regulations, we are studying also its recommendations, [I'm not sure about this part. We can't guarantee we can comply with all the regulations since we don't even know them well but maybe we shouldn't say "most".]and we have trained our employees involved in managing information from players, like customer service, to answer to our users request following the new EU updates. You can always access your information through our customer service emails for each game or region or by sending an email to cs@boyaa.com
3.Information We Collect and How We Collect It
Information About You That We Get From Connected Third-Party Applications, Including Social Networks (like Facebook)
(If you live in the EU zone some of this policies might be enhanced and improved. Go to section 2 to get more information about the European GDPR)
If you play Boyaa's games or access any of our other Services on connected third-party applications or connect our Services to any third-party applications, including social networks like Facebook, Boyaa may receive certain information about you from the provider of the third-party application. The information we receive depends on the Boyaa game you're playing, the third-party application, your privacy settings and, if applicable, your friends' privacy settings on that third-party application.
For example, Boyaa may collect and store some or all of the following information shared by the provider of the connected third-party application:
â€¢	your first and last name;
â€¢	your profile picture or its URL;
â€¢	your user ID number (like your Facebook ID number), which may be linked to publicly-available information like your name and profile photo;
â€¢	the user ID number and other public data for your friends;
â€¢	the login e-mail you provided to that third-party application when you registered with it;
â€¢	your physical location and that of the devices you use to access our Services;
â€¢	your gender;
â€¢	your birthday and/or age range;
â€¢	information about your activities on or through the connected third-party application;
â€¢	other publicly-available information on the third-party application; and/or
â€¢	any other information that you or the provider of the third-party application share with Boyaa.
If you access our Services from a third-party application or connect our Services to a third-party application, you should also read that third-party application's Terms of Service and Privacy Policy.
If you are unclear about what information a third-party application is sharing with us, please go to the third-party application to find out more about their privacy practices.
Cookies and Automated Information Collection
We and service providers acting on our behalf, like Google Analytics, store log files and use tracking technologies such as:
â€¢	cookies, which are small pieces of data transferred to your mobile device or computer for record-keeping purposes;
â€¢	web beacons, which let us know if a certain page was visited or whether an e-mail was opened;
â€¢	tracking pixels, which allow us or our advertising partners to advertise more efficiently and effectively;
â€¢	local shared objects, also known as flash cookies, which help us to reduce fraud, remember your in-game preferences and speed up load times.
We and our service providers use these log files, tags, and tracking technologies to collect and analyze certain kinds of technical information, including:
â€¢	IP addresses;
â€¢	the type of computer or mobile device you are using;
â€¢	your operating system version;
â€¢	your mobile device's identifiers, like your MAC Address, Identifier For Advertising (IDFA), and/or International Mobile Equipment Identity (IMEI);
â€¢	your browser types;
â€¢	your browser language;
â€¢	referring and exit pages, and URLs;
â€¢	platform type;
â€¢	the number of clicks on a page or feature;
â€¢	domain names;
â€¢	landing pages;
â€¢	pages viewed and the order of those pages;
â€¢	the amount of time spent on particular pages;
â€¢	game state and the date and time of activity on our websites or games.
In some cases, we will connect this information with your social network ID or Boyaa user ID.
Other Information from Your Mobile Device
If you play Boyaa games on your mobile device, in addition to your device identifiers, we may also collect:
â€¢	the name you have associated with your device;
â€¢	your telephone number;
â€¢	your country; and
â€¢	your specific geolocation;
â€¢	your mobile contacts (as further described below in "Information About Your Contacts"); and
â€¢	information about Boyaa and other third-party apps you have on your device.
Information About You That You Share With Us Directly
When you use our Services (whether through a social network or through Boyaa directly), you may give us information directly (like when you're setting up your account) and we will store that on our systems and use it for the purposes described in this Privacy Policy.
Some games or parts of our Services may use a more traditional registration or account set-up process where you may be asked to give us some or all of the following information:
â€¢	your age or birthday;
â€¢	your first and last names;
â€¢	your e-mail address;
â€¢	a password; and
â€¢	other information that helps us make sure it's you accessing your account or helps us improve our services.
We may also let you create a player profile, separate from your social networking site profile (for example, your Facebook profile), that other Boyaa players can see. Your player profile may include information like:
â€¢	a profile photo;
â€¢	game username(s);
â€¢	your gender;
â€¢	biographic details (like your age or age range);
â€¢	approximate location information that you provide;
â€¢	links to your profiles on various social network;
â€¢	details about the games you play; and
â€¢	a Boyaa player ID number that is created by Boyaa and used to identify your profile.
Certain information in your Boyaa profile may be publicly accessible on Boyaa's websites that offer direct access to Boyaa games, including:
â€¢	The Boyaa player ID;
â€¢	Your first and last names; and
â€¢	Your player profile picture.
Except for games designed for children under 13, your Boyaa player ID number used to identify your account and player profile will appear in the URL of your profile page. It will only allow access to information you make public in your settings.
Information About Your Contacts
We may give you the ability to import your address book contacts or manually enter them so that you can locate your contacts on Boyaa and invite them to join you in our games or other aspects of our Services. You are responsible for getting your contacts' permission when you opt to give their contact details to us. We may also get information about you from other Boyaa users importing or entering their contacts. We use and may store this contact information to help you and your contacts connect through our Services. If you want to remove your contacts stored by us, follow the instructions provided in the game to request that we remove them from our systems. If you need to enter a password to allow us to access your address book, we will not store that password.
Information You Generate Using Our Communications Features
Except for games designed for children under 13, you may be able to take part in certain activities on our Service that let you communicate or share information not just with Boyaa, but also with other Boyaa players. These include:
â€¢	participating in player forums and message boards;
â€¢	posting public comments to other players' profiles or gameboards;
â€¢	sending private messages or invitations to other players, either directly on our websites or to their e-mail accounts;
â€¢	chatting with other players; and/or
â€¢	posting photos or drawings.
You acknowledge and expressly agree that we may access in real-time, record and/or store archives of these communications, comments, photos and drawings on Boyaa's servers to make use of them to protect the safety and well-being of our players and Boyaa's rights and property in connection with our Services; to conduct research; to operate, improve, personalize and optimize our Services and our players' experiences, including through the use of analytics; and to manage and deliver contextual advertising.
Payment Information
If you purchase a license to use in-game virtual currency or virtual items in a game you play on Boyaa.com, our third-party payment processor will collect the billing and financial information it needs to process your charges. This may include your postal address, e-mail address and financial information. Boyaa does not collect or store your financial information, like credit card numbers. However, Boyaa's payment processors may share non-financial information with us related to your purchases, like your name, billing address and the items purchased in order to fulfill your order. Boyaa may also obtain the billing and payment information that you provide when your purchase is processed by someone else (like Facebook, Apple or Google) such as when you purchase something in a game you play on a social network or that you downloaded on your mobile device. Our Terms of Service explain our policies and terms relevant to our charges, billing practices, third-party credits and virtual currencies. Please note that purchases of third party credits or currencies may also be subject to those parties' policies.
Customer Support Correspondence
Except as provided herein, when you ask for help from our Customer Support team, we will collect and store the contact information you give them (generally, your name and e-mail address), information about your game play or activity on our Services, and your Boyaa player and/or social network ID number. We will also store the communications you have with the Customer Service team and any information in those communications in order to provide support and improve the Services. For users of our games designed for children under 13, we will use your contact information for the sole purpose of providing a one-time response to your question. We will then delete your information from our servers.
Information You Give Us For Text Messaging Services
We receive and store the information you provide, including your mobile telephone number, when you choose to sign up to receive SMS messages.
Other Sources
We may collect or receive information about you from other sources like third-party information providers. We use this information along with information you provide us directly, for example, to help you and your friends connect or to serve you advertising more tailored to your interests.
4.How We Use the Information We Collect
The main use of the information we collect and store is to provide a better gaming experience, but there are other uses as well. The uses for which we collect and store your information include:
â€¢	to operate, improve and optimize our Services and our players' experiences;
â€¢	to create your game accounts and allow you to play our games;
â€¢	to identify and suggest connections with other Boyaa players and personalize our Services to you;
â€¢	to enable players to communicate with each other;
â€¢	to provide technical support and respond to player inquiries;
â€¢	to protect the safety and well-being of our players;
â€¢	to protect Boyaa's rights and property in connection with our Services;
â€¢	to prevent fraud or potentially illegal activities, and to enforce our Terms of Service;
â€¢	to manage and deliver contextual and behavioral advertising;
â€¢	to notify players of in-game updates, new products or promotional offers;
â€¢	to administer rewards, surveys, sweepstakes, contests, or other promotional activities or events sponsored or managed by us or our business partners;
â€¢	to comply with our legal obligations, resolve any disputes we may have with you or other players, and to enforce our agreements with third parties; and
â€¢	to conduct research.
One important use of your information is communication. If you have provided your e-mail address to Boyaa, we will use it to respond to customer support inquiries, and keep you informed of your in-game activity, including comments from friends, let you know about in-game status such as "crops ready" as well as tell you about gift and neighbor requests. Some messages, like invites for friends to join you in a game, may include your name and profile photo. We may also send promotional e-mail messages and promotional SMS messages (e.g. text messages) ("Promotional Communications") directly or in partnership with other parties, in accordance with your marketing preferences. Each Promotional Communication will offer you choices about receiving additional messages. Receipt of such communications depends on Boyaa having certain contact information from you. If you play one of our games designed for children under 13, you will not be able to provide us with certain contact information. Please see the section on Our Policies Concerning Children for more information.
5.How We Share Your Information
We may disclose or publish aggregated information and other non-personal information about our players for industry analysis, demographic profiling, marketing, analytics, advertising, and other business purposes.
In addition, we may share your information (which may include personal information) with third parties (in other words, parties other than Boyaa) or allow third parties to collect this information from our Services in the following circumstances:
Your Consent
With your consent, we may share your information with third parties or allow them to collect your information from our Services in some ways not specifically described in this Privacy Policy.
Friends and Other Boyaa Players
The Service supports and often encourages you to interact with other players. In most Boyaa games, if you play through a social network or register through a social network (for example, Facebook Connect), your social network friends will see your name, profile photo and descriptions of your game activity. Similarly, in many Boyaa games, other players, regardless of whether they are your social network friends or not, will be able to see descriptions of your game activity (including the identification of any Boyaa games you have played), communicate with you within our Services, and view your game profile, which may include your name or a "game name" and your profile photo. For example, in Boyaa Poker, any other player may see your game profile if you are playing at the same table. In certain cases, your profile photo can reveal your social network ID or Boyaa player ID, and access to a social network ID or Boyaa player ID may allow others to view the public information associated with your related social network profile or Boyaa account. Other players may also be able to send you game requests or even friend requests through the related social network's or Boyaa's communication channels.
Safety, Security and Compliance with Law
Your information, and the contents of all of your online communications in our Services and between You and Boyaa may be accessed and monitored as needed to provide our Service and may be disclosed:
â€¢	when we have a good faith belief that we have to disclose the information in response to lawful requests by public authorities, including to meet national security or law enforcement requirements, or legal process (for example, a court order, search warrant or subpoena);
â€¢	to satisfy any laws or regulations that apply;
â€¢	where we believe in our sole discretion that the Service is being used in committing a crime, including to report such criminal activity or to share information with other companies and organizations for the purposes of fraud protection, credit risk reduction, and other security precautions;
â€¢	when we have a good faith belief that there is an emergency that poses a threat to the health and/or safety of you, another person or the public generally; and
â€¢	to protect the rights or property of Boyaa and other applicable third parties, including to enforce our Terms of Service.
Third-Party Service Providers
We will share your information with third-party companies to perform services on our behalf, like processing payments, analyzing data, optimizing game play, e-mail delivery, hosting services, customer service and to help us in our marketing efforts, including managing and delivering contextual and tailored advertisements. We contractually require these third-party service providers to maintain the confidentiality of the information we share with them, and we contractually require them not use your information for anything other than to provide services on our behalf.
Sale or Merger
In the event that Boyaa undergoes a business transition (including proposed transactions), like a merger, acquisition by another company, or sale of all or part its assets (like selling a game), we may disclose or transfer all of your information, including personal information, to the successor organization in the transition. We will make reasonable efforts to let you and other players know (in the way described in Changes to Our Privacy Policy) of the business transition before transferring your personal information.
6.How to Access, Update and Manage Your Information
(If you live in the EU zone some of this policies might be enhanced and improved. Go to section 2 to get more information about the European GDPR)
Information We Receive From a Third-Party Application Where You Play Our Games or From Your Mobile Device
To manage the information Boyaa receives about you from a third-party application where you play our games, like Facebook, you will need to follow the instructions for the third-party application for updating your information and changing your privacy settings. The privacy management tools for applications on Facebook can be found here. To review and update information associated with your Boyaa game profile in certain games, visit the "settings" page in that game. You also can manage some aspects of information collection and use by visiting the "settings" page of your mobile device and reviewing the permissions of each application or "app."
Once Boyaa receives your information from a third-party application or your mobile device, that information is stored and used by Boyaa in accordance with this Privacy Policy. You may access and update that information as described below.
Accessing and Updating Your Information Held by Boyaa
If you want to review, delete, or change the information Boyaa has about you or have additional questions, e-mail us at cs@boyaa.com.
Stopping Use of Your Information
If you no longer want Boyaa to make active use of your information, you may send an e-mail to cs@boyaa.com. Place "Delete My Account" in the subject line and include your first name, last name, e-mail address and your social network ID for the social network from which you access our Services (if applicable) in the body of the e-mail (for example, your Facebook user ID). We will respond to your request within thirty days. Please note that certain records, for example those relating to payments or customer service matters, will be held for legal and accounting purposes. If you have sent content through or posted content on the Service, we may not be able to delete it.
Opting Out of Geolocation
If you have previously allowed us to access your geolocation data, you can stop making geolocation available to us by visiting your mobile device's settings for the relevant application or the "settings" page for the relevant game.
Opting Out of Ongoing Collection of Information About Non-Boyaa Apps You Have On Your Device
To the extent that one of our games is collecting information about non-Boyaa apps you have on your device, the game will provide you with an option to stop making that information available to us in the "settings" page for the relevant game.
Opting Out of Promotional Emails from Boyaa
If you want to stop receiving promotional e-mails from Boyaa, click on the "unsubscribe" link in any promotional email from Boyaa or visit the e-mail preference page. Please note that once we receive your request, it may take an additional period of time for your opt-out to become effective. Your unsubscribe or e-mail preference change will be processed promptly, and in no event longer than ten business days.
Opting Out of Other Communications
You can opt out of receiving SMS messages (for example, text messages) by texting back STOP to the number we send the text from for that particular SMS message program. In some cases a preferences management page will also be available. When we receive an opt-out message from you for SMS messages, we may send a message confirming our receipt of your opt-out.
When you install our apps on your mobile device you can choose to receive push notifications, which are messages an app sends you on your mobile device even when the app is not on. You can turn off notifications by visiting your mobile device's "settings" page.
Opting Out of Cookie Tracking
You can set your web browser to warn you about attempts to place cookies on your computer or limit the type of cookies you allow. Flash cookies operate differently than browser cookies and cookie management tools available in a web browser may not remove flash cookies. To learn more about and manage flash cookies you can visit the Adobe website and make changes at the Global Privacy Settings Panel.
If you disable cookies, you may lose some of the features and functionality of our Services because Boyaa cookies are necessary to track and enhance your game activities.
7.Privacy Policies of Linked Third-Party Services and Advertisers
Our websites and games may contain advertisements from Third-Party Services, which are companies other than Boyaa that may link to their own websites, online services or mobile applications. We are not responsible for the privacy practices or the content of these Third-Party Services. If you have any questions about how these Third-Party Services use your information, you should review their policies and contact them directly.
8.Our Policies Concerning Children
Most of our websites and games are not for children under the age of 13 and we do not knowingly collect any personal information from children under 13. Children under 13 should not use these websites or games at any time. If we learn that we have inadvertently gathered personal information from a child under 13, we will take reasonable measures to promptly remove that information from our records.
Boyaa provides education games, like Words with Friends EDU, which are intended to be enjoyed by parents, teachers, and children of all ages. Boyaa may also provide games like Looney Tunes Dash, which are intended for users of all ages. In these games, Boyaa does not knowingly collect personal information (as that term is defined under the Children's Online Privacy Protection Act (COPPA)) from users under the age of 13, except as permitted by COPPA. For example, Boyaa may collect persistent identifiers to support the internal operations of its games. If Boyaa learns that a child under the age of 13 has provided us with personal information that is not subject to a COPPA exception, Boyaa will delete such information.
9.How Long We Keep Your Information
(If you live in the EU zone some of this policies might be enhanced and improved. Go to section 2 to get more information about the European GDPR)
How long we retain your information depends on why we collected it and how we use it. We will not retain your personal information for longer than is necessary for our business purposes or for legal requirements. For instance, we may retain some information for a few years after you have closed your account with us if this is necessary to meet our legal obligations or to exercise, defend or establish legal rights.
10.Security of Your Information
We implement security measures to help protect the security of your information both online and offline. We take steps to ensure that your data is treated securely and in accordance with this Privacy Policy. These measures vary based upon the sensitivity of your information.
If you have an account registered directly with Boyaa, your profile information is protected by the password you use to access your Boyaa account. It is important that you protect and maintain your Boyaa account's security and that you immediately tell us of any unauthorized use of your account. If you forget the password to your Boyaa account, the Service allows you to request that instructions be sent to you that explain how to reset your password. If you access our Services through a social network and your social network account is hacked, this may lead to someone playing your Boyaa games without your permission. So, be careful to keep your social network account information, including your social network account password, secure as well. We urge you to log out of your Boyaa account and any social network account you have used to access our Services after you use it.
When you sign into your Boyaa account or enter payment information, we or our third party payment processor use encryption to transmit that information.
While we take precautions against possible security breaches of our Services and our customer databases and records, no website or Internet transmission is completely secure. We cannot guarantee that unauthorized access, hacking, data loss, or other breaches will never occur, and we cannot guarantee the security of your information while it is being transmitted to our Service. Any transmission is at your own risk. If you have questions about the security of our websites, please contact us at cs@boyaa.com.
11.Changes to Our Privacy Policy
If we decide to make material changes to our Privacy Policy, we will tell you and other players by placing a notice on Boyaa.com or its equivalent in-game, or by sending you a notice to the e-mail address we have on file for you prior to the change becoming effective. We may supplement this process by placing notices on game blogs, social network pages, and/or forums and on other Boyaa websites. You should periodically check www.boyaa.com and this privacy page for updates.
12.Contact Us
For any questions about its Privacy Policy or any other issue please contact Boyaa at: cs@boyaa.com

4. à¸à¸²à¸£à¹€à¸Šà¸·à¹ˆà¸­à¸¡à¹‚à¸¢à¸‡

5. à¸à¸²à¸£à¹€à¸›à¸¥à¸µà¹ˆà¸¢à¸™ à¸«à¸£à¸·à¸­ à¸à¸²à¸£à¸¥à¸šà¸‚à¹‰à¸­à¸¡à¸¹à¸¥à¸‚à¸­à¸‡à¸„à¸¸à¸“

Privasi&Ketentuan Layanan
Polis Privasi Boya
Tanggal berlaku : 25 Mungkin 2009
Boya Interactive International Limited dan anggota-anggotanya, termasuk di dalamnya tanpa terkecuali, Boya Online Game Development (Shenzhen) Co.,Ltd. dan Shenzhen Dong fang Boya Technology Co.,Ltd. (tergabung, â€œBoyaâ€ or â€œusâ€ or â€œweâ€) diresmikan untuk melindungi hak privasi dari pengguna online kita (â€œuserâ€ or â€œyouâ€). Polis Privasi Online ini (â€œPrivacy Policyâ€) telah dirancang untuk memberitahu Anda sebagai menuju jalan di mana kita mengumpulkan, menyimpan, menggunakan, memperlihatkan, dan mengatur informasi yang Anda sediakan dalam berhubungan dengan Boya game, aplikasi, atau website (â€œServiceâ€). Silakan catat bahwa jangkauan dari Polis Privasi ini adalah terbatas hanya untuk informasi yang dikumpulkan dari Boya melalui penggunaan layanan tersebut.
Dengan menggunakan layanan tersebut, Anda menyetujui kumpulan dan penggunaan dari informasi personal Anda sebagai penggarisan di Polis Privasi ini. Kita mungkin mengubah Polis Privasi tersebut sekali dalam suatu waktu. [Jika kita membuat perubahan mendasar dari Polis Privasi kita, kita akan mengirim pengumuman di website kami], dan kita menganjurkan Anda untuk memeriksa Polis Privasi tersebut secara teratur. Jika Anda tidak setuju pada Polis ini atau versi perubahan apa saja mengenai Polis ini, maka Anda tidak harus menggunakan layanan tersebut.
1. Informasi yang Anda sediakan untuk kita Tujuan utama Boya dalam pengumpulan informasi pengguna adalah untuk menyediakan dan meningkatkan layanan dan untuk membolehkan pengguna untuk menavigasi dan menikmati layanan dengan mudah.
Kita mungkin mengumpulkan informasi identifikasi non personal tentang pengguna kapan saja mereka menggunakan satu atau beberapa dari layanan tersebut. Informasi identifikasi non-personal mungkin mencakup nama Anda, tipe computer dan informasi teknis mengenai maksud pengguna dalam berhubungan dengan Site kami, seperti sistem operasi dan layanan internet yang menyediakan kegunaan dan informasi lain yang mirip.
Ketika Anda menggunakan satu atau beberapa dai layanan, kita mungkin mengumpulkan dan merekam informasi yang Anda sediakan secara sukarela sesuai dengan Polis tersebut. Tipe informasi personal dikumpulkan sesuai dengan daftar aktivitas di atas mungkin berbeda-beda tergantung pada aktivitas. Informasi personal ini diartikan sebagai informasi tentang Anda yang digunakan untuk menghubungi atau mengidentifikasi Anda. Informasi personal mungkin mencakup: 1) nama Anda, (2) nomor identifikasi Anda, atau (3) alamat email. Sebagai tambahan, kita mungkin membutuhkan informasi dari Anda melalui (1) Akses dan partisipasi Anda dalam papan pesan pada layanan (2) email Anda tentang pertanyaan untuk bantuan langganan kami atau (3) pembelian Anda tentang barang virtual dengan berbagai tipe. Silakan catat itu karena bagian pihak ketiga mengatur pembelian barang virtual yang ditawarkan oleh layanan tersebut, kami tidak memiliki akses ke detail kredit dan informasi billing Anda, dan kita menganjurkan Anda untuk melihat kembali polis asuransi pihak ketiga tentang layanan pembelian tentang barang virtual. Boya juga mungkin mengundang Anda untuk membagi informasi non personal tentang Anda sendiri yang mungkin mencakup tetapi tidak terbatas pada: (1) umur atau tanggal kelahiran Anda; (2) jenis kelamin Anda; (3) tipe hardware dan informasi teknis mengenai maksud pengguna dalam berhubungan dengan layanan, seperti sistem operasi dan layanan internet yang menyediakan kegunaan dan informasi lain yang serupa dengan itu; (4) website favorit Anda, informasi teman dan halaman fans (secara terkumpul ditujukan sebagai informasi non personal). Jika informasi non personal dikumpulkan untuk sebuah aktivitas yang juga memerlukan informasi personal, Boya mungkin menggabungkan informasi non personal Anda dengan informasi personal Anda sebagai usaha untuk menyediakan kepada Anda dengan pengalaman pengguna yang lebih baik, untuk meningkatkan kualitas dan nilai layanan dan untuk menganalisa bagaimana layanan digunakan. Sebagai tambahan, kita mungkin mengumpulkan, menyimpan, menggunakan, memperlihatkan, dan mengatur informasi apa saja yang dikenal tidak secara personal tanpa pembatasan dan mungkin membuat dan menggunakan analisis, models, dan produk kerja yang lain berdasarkan pada penggabungan infomasi personal dan non personal tanpa pembatasan, penyediaan beberapa kegunaan yang mengidentifikasi Anda harus ditentukan oleh Polis Privasi ini.
Layanan tersebut juga akan merekam informasi bermain game, mencakup tanpa pembatasan, skor tertinggi Anda atau durasi sesi game.
Sebagai tambahan untuk pengumpulan informasi dari penjelasan di atas, Anda mungkin memilih untuk membagi informasi tambahan tentang Anda sendiri melalui layanan, seperti dalam game atau di papan pesan. Apa saja aksi yang Anda tunjukan dengan pemain lain dianggap public, dan diberikan sebagai satu-satunya diskresi Anda.
2. Informasi yang dikumpulkan dari penggunaan Anda terhadap layanan Kapan saja Anda mengakses layanan, kita mungkin mengumpulkan sejumlah informasi mencakup tetapi tidak terbatas pada alamat protocol internet, tipe browser, bahasa browser, halaman yang mengarahkan / mengeluarkan dan URLs, tipe platform, nomor klik, nama domain, halaman mendarat, halaman yang ditampilkan dan pesanan atas halaman-halaman itu, sejumlah waktu yang dihabiskan dalam halaman khusus, dan tanggal dan waktu dari aktivitas ini. Kita menggunakan informasi ini untuk penyesuaian yang lebih baik layanan untuk keuntungan Anda, untuk menyediakan kepada Anda bantuan langganan yang lebih efisien, dan meningkatkan keseluruhan layanan.
Kita mungkin menggunakan cookies dan teknologi lain untuk menyediakan kepada Anda dengan isi langganan dan untuk meningkatkan efisiensi dari interaksi Anda dengan layanan. Sebuah cookie adalah sebuah file data kecil yang kami transfer ke hard disk computer Anda, secara umum untuk mengenal pengguna computer secara cepat dan untuk mengingat hal-hal tentang kunjungan pengguna, seperti preferensi Anda atau nama pengguna dan password. Layanan mengirimkan cookies ke computer Anda ketika Anda mengakses atau melihat isi dari game Boya. Informasi di dalam sebuah cookie mungkin dihubungkan ke informasi personal dengan tujuan seperti meningkatkan kualitas dari layanan kita, menyesuaikan rekomendasi dengan keuntungan Anda, dan membuat layanan dapat lebih mudah digunakan. Anda dapat melarang kegunaan cookies kapan saja Anda mau, walaupun Anda mungkin tidak dapat mengakses atau menggunakan keistimewaan dari layanan. Ketika Anda menggunakan sebuah lokasi â€“ membolehkan layanan, kita mungkin mengumpulkan dan memproses informasi tentang lokasi nyata Anda, mencakup waktu nyata dari lokasi geografi dalam mobile device Anda di mana Anda menggunakan internet. Data lokasi ini dikumpulkan tanpa nama dalam sebuah bentuk yang tidak secara personal mengidentifikasi Anda dan digunakan oleh kita untuk menyediakan dan meningkatkan lokasi â€“ berdasarkan produk dan layanan.
3. Pengungkapan informasi personal Anda Sewaktu-waktu, kita mungkin membuat informasi personal yang terpercaya tersedia untuk strategi partner kita dan orang lainnya yang menyediakan kepada kita layanan ( seperti informasi memproses dan mengabulkan perintah pengguna) atau untuk membantu pemasaran kita ke langganan. Informasi personal semacam itu akan dibagi kepada pihak-pihak ini saja untuk menyediakan atau meningkatkan produk dan layanan kita. Di dalam kasus dalam akses dan pengumpulan data, informasi yang Anda sediakan tidak akan diperlihatkan, disewakan, dikontrak, dipinjam, dijual, atau sebaliknya secara sukarela didistribusikan kepada pihak ketiga lainnya kecuali pihak anggota Boya dan akan digunakan semata-mata untuk tujuan menyediakan kepada Anda dengan dan peningkatan layanan.Anda mengerti dan setuju bahwa kami mungkin dibutuhkan untuk mengungkapkan informasi personal jika dibutuhkan untuk dilakukan oleh hukum atau dalam keadaan itikad baik percaya bahwa pengungkapan semacam itu adalah diperlukan secara beralasan untuk menghindari tanggung jawab, untuk memenuhi proses hukum, mencakup tetapi tidak terbatas kepada sebagai jaminan penyelidikan, panggilan ke pengadilan, UU, atau perintah pengadilan, atau untuk melindungi hak dan properti kami, atau itu untuk public. Catat bahwa Boya tidak wajib untuk menyangsikan atau menentang keabsahan dari jaminan penyelidikan, panggilan ke pengadilan, atau permintaan pemerintah yang serupa yang mungkin diterima Boya. Sebagai tambahan, dalam situasi penggabungan, penerimaan, reorganisasi, bangkrut, atau situasi lain yang serupa, informasi langganan mungkin ditransfer kepada pengganti atau petugas Boya, jika diizinkan oleh dan dilakukan sesuai dengan hukum yang berlaku.
4. Hubungan Layanan mungkin berisi links ke website lain. Kenyataan bahwa link layanan ke sebuah website atau menampilkan sebuah iklan atau tipe periklanan yang lain tidak berarti bahwa Boya berkuasa atau berwenang bahwa pihak ketiga, maupun itu adalah perwakilan dari anggota kami dengan pihak ketiga itu. Boya tidak bertanggung jawab terhadap polis privasi dari website lain di mana Anda pilih untuk diakses dari layanan. Silakan pastikan untuk membaca polis privasi dari website-website itu ketika meninggalkan layanan.
5. Perubahan atau penghapusan informasi Anda Anda mungkin menampilkan ulang, mengupdate, membetulkan atau menghapus satu atau beebrapa informasi dengan mengubah informasi yang berlaku di halaman profil Anda. Jika Anda menghapus seluruh informasi secara lengkap, akun Anda mungkin menjadi dinonaktifkan. Jika Anda menginginkan kita untuk menghapus rekaman Anda dalam sistem kami, silakan hubungi kami dan kami akan berusaha untuk mengakomodasi permintaan Anda jika kita tidak berkewajiban secara hukum untuk mempertahankan rekaman.
6. Keamanan Kita harus meletakkan di tempatnya secara beralasan tindakan teknik, fisik, administratif, dan organisasional yang dirancang untuk mengamankan informasi personal anda dari kerugian kecelakaan dan dari pengaksesan, penggunaan, pengubahan, atau pengungkapan yang tidak sah. Bagaimanapun, kita tidak dapat menjamin atau menggunakan informasi personal Anda untuk tujuan yang tidak patut. Dan juga silakan catat bahwa email dan sistem pesan dan metode enkripsi lain seperti channel komunikasi jaminan SSL tidak dianggap aman, jadi kita tidak menganjurkan kepada Anda pengiriman informasi personal melalui metode ini. Anda bertanggung jawab terhadap informasi personal yang Anda sampaikan dalam hal ini.
7. Anak-anak Kita mengkhawatirkan privasi anak-anak yang menggunakan internet. Kita tidak mengumpulkan informasi personal dai anak-anak di bawah umur 13 tahun. Jika kami mempelajari bahwa kita telah mengumpulkan informasi personal dari anak-anak di bawah 13 tahun secara tidak hati-hati, atau jika Anda sadar dan memberitahu kami bahwa seorang anak di bawah 13 tahun telah menyediakan informasi personal untuk kami, kami akan mengambil langkah untuk menghapus informasi tersebut secepat mungkin.
8. Hukum Pemerintah Polis privasi ini dan penggunaan Anda terhadap layanan diperintah oleh hukum Hong Kong. Segala perselisihan di antara kami berhubungan dengan polis ini atau penggunaan Anda terhadap bagian ini harus diselesaikan semata-mata di CIETAC yang berlokasi di Shenzhen China.
9. Penggunaan Internasional Polis Privasi ini dimaksudkan untuk sejalan dengan hukum dan peraturan Hong Kong, dan kami tidak menargetkan pengguna di luar Hong Kong dan tidak menuntut bahwa website kami tepat dan sesuai hukum untuk digunakan atau diakses di luar Hong Kong. Jika Anda mengakses website kami dari luar Hong Kong, Anda melakukannya dengan resiko sendii. Anda adalah satu-satunya yang bertanggung jawab untuk memenuhi seluruh hukum lokal, aturan, dan peraturan berkenaan dengan tingkah laku online dan akses website.
10. Persetujuan Dengan mengirim data Anda, Anda secara eksplisit mengizinkan pentransferan dan pernyimpanan ke database kita tetap dengan klausul dari polis privasi ini.
11. Hubungi kami Jika Anda mempunyai pertanyaan tentang Polis Privasi ini, silakan hubungi kami.
